Milan">A.C. Milan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> Moreover, their sponsored national teams include <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a>, <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_football_team" title="Mexico national football team">Mexico</a>, <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sweden_national_football_team" title="Sweden national football team">Sweden</a>, <a href="/wiki/Japan_national_football_team" title="Japan national football team">Japan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Russia_national_football_team" title="Russia national football team">Russia</a>.\n</p><p>Adidas has sponsored numerous players, including <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kak%C3%A1" title="Kak\xc3\xa1">Kak\xc3\xa1</a>, <a href="/wiki/David_Beckham" title="David Beckham">David Beckham</a>, <a href="/wiki/Steven_Gerrard" title="Steven Gerrard">Steven Gerrard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gareth_Bale" title="Gareth Bale">Gareth Bale</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thomas_M%C3%BCller" title="Thomas M\xc3\xbcller">Thomas M\xc3\xbcller</a>, <a href="/wiki/Xavi" title="Xavi">Xavi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mesut_%C3%96zil" title="Mesut \xc3\x96zil">Mesut \xc3\x96zil</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_Rodr%C3%ADguez" title="James Rodr\xc3\xadguez">James Rodr\xc3\xadguez</a>, <a href="/wiki/Iker_Casillas" title="Iker Casillas">Iker Casillas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arjen_Robben" title="Arjen Robben">Arjen Robben</a>, <a href="/wiki/Paul_Pogba" title="Paul Pogba">Paul Pogba</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dele_Alli" title="Dele Alli">Dele Alli</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luis_Su%C3%A1rez" title="Luis Su\xc3\xa1rez">Luis Su\xc3\xa1rez</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ivan_Rakiti%C4%87" title="Ivan Rakiti\xc4\x87">Ivan Rakiti\xc4\x87</a>, <a href="/wiki/Diego_Costa" title="Diego Costa">Diego Costa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Salah" title="Mohamed Salah">Mohamed Salah</a>, <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Firmino" title="Roberto Firmino">Roberto Firmino</a> and <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Neuer" title="Manuel Neuer">Manuel Neuer</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Adidas is one of the official sponsors of the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Adidas_Finale" title="Adidas Finale">Adidas Finale</a> is the competition\'s official match ball.<sup id="cite_ref-adidas_Finale_Munich_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-adidas_Finale_Munich-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Along with the aforementioned <a href="/wiki/Adidas_Predator" title="Adidas Predator">Adidas Predator</a> boot, Adidas manufactures the <a href="/wiki/AdiPure" title="AdiPure">adiPure</a> range of football boots. Adidas provides clothing and equipment for all teams in <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Soccer" title="Major League Soccer">Major League Soccer</a> (MLS).\n</p><p>In July 2014, Adidas and Manchester United agreed to a ten-year kit deal, beginning with the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Premier_League" title="2015\xe2\x80\x9316 Premier League">2015\xe2\x80\x9316 Premier League season</a>. This kit deal has a guaranteed minimum value of \xc2\xa3750&#160;million (US$1.29&#160;billion), making it the most valuable kit deal in sports history, and replaced rival <a href="/wiki/Nike,_Inc." title="Nike, Inc.">Nike</a> as the club\'s global equipment partner.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Andy_murray_crop.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Andy_murray_crop.JPG/170px-Andy_murray_crop.JPG" width="170" height="254" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Andy_murray_crop.JPG/255px-Andy_murray_crop.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f8/Andy_murray_crop.JPG 2x" data-file-width="334" data-file-height="499" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Andy_murray_crop.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Andy_Murray" title="Andy Murray">Andy Murray</a> endorsed Adidas from the start of the 2010 season until the end of the <a href="/wiki/2014_Andy_Murray_tennis_season" title="2014 Andy Murray tennis season">2014 season</a> receiving US$4.9&#160;million per year.</div></div></div>\n<p>In November 2009, World Number 4 tennis player <a href="/wiki/Andy_Murray" title="Andy Murray">Andy Murray</a> was confirmed as Adidas\' highest-paid star with a five-year contract reportedly worth US$24.5&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> In <a href="/wiki/Cincinnati" title="Cincinnati">Cincinnati</a>, at the <a href="/wiki/Association_of_Tennis_Professionals" title="Association of Tennis Professionals">ATP Tennis Tournament</a> in Mason, they have also sponsored the <a href="/wiki/Ball_boy#Tennis" title="Ball boy">ball-boy and ball-girl</a> uniforms. Adidas is also partners with Malibu Tennis Camp, Green Fitness GmbH and with Sch\xc3\xb6ler &amp; Micke Sportartikel Vertriebs GmbH.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Adidas has sponsored numerous basketball players past and present like <a href="/wiki/Kareem_Abdul-Jabbar" title="Kareem Abdul-Jabbar">Kareem Abdul-Jabbar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tracy_McGrady" title="Tracy McGrady">Tracy McGrady</a>, as well as <a href="/wiki/Chauncey_Billups" title="Chauncey Billups">Chauncey Billups</a>, <a href="/wiki/Derrick_Rose" title="Derrick Rose">Derrick Rose</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brandon_Knight_(basketball)" title="Brandon Knight (basketball)">Brandon Knight</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eric_Gordon" title="Eric Gordon">Eric Gordon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Josh_Smith" title="Josh Smith">Josh Smith</a>, <a href="/wiki/Damian_Lillard" title="Damian Lillard">Damian Lillard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Wiggins" title="Andrew Wiggins">Andrew Wiggins</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tim_Duncan" title="Tim Duncan">Tim Duncan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jeremy_Lin" title="Jeremy Lin">Jeremy Lin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Iman_Shumpert" title="Iman Shumpert">Iman Shumpert</a>, <a href="/wiki/John_Wall_(basketball)" title="John Wall (basketball)">John Wall</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nick_Young_(basketball)" title="Nick Young (basketball)">Nick Young</a>. Adidas endorsed <a href="/wiki/Kobe_Bryant" title="Kobe Bryant">Kobe Bryant</a> with the Adidas Equipment KB8 as his first signature shoe until July 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> The company also endorsed <a href="/wiki/Kevin_Garnett" title="Kevin Garnett">Kevin Garnett</a> until he opted out of his contract in 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Gilbert_Arenas" title="Gilbert Arenas">Gilbert Arenas</a> was an Adidas endorser until 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> In August 2015, <a href="/wiki/James_Harden" title="James Harden">James Harden</a> left Nike for Adidas by signing a 13-year contract reportedly worth US$200&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/Rugby_union" title="Rugby union">rugby union</a>, Adidas is the current kit supplier to the <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_national_rugby_union_team" title="New Zealand national rugby union team">All Blacks</a>, the <a href="/wiki/France_national_rugby_union_team" title="France national rugby union team">France national team</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Italian_national_rugby_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Italian national rugby team">Italian national rugby team</a> and the South African <a href="/wiki/Stormers" title="Stormers">Stormers</a> and <a href="/wiki/Western_Province_(rugby_team)" title="Western Province (rugby team)">Western Province</a> rugby union teams among others. Adidas is also the <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_Rugby_Union" class="mw-redirect" title="New Zealand Rugby Union">New Zealand Rugby Union</a> clothing sponsor and supplies clothing to all <a href="/wiki/Super_Rugby" title="Super Rugby">Super Rugby</a> franchises, a selection of domestic teams and national referees. Adidas are also the official match ball supplier to the <a href="/wiki/Heineken_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Heineken Cup">Heineken Cup</a>. Adidas was the <a href="/wiki/British_and_Irish_Lions" title="British and Irish Lions">British and Irish Lions</a> kit supplier from 1997 to 2013. They are the jersey manufacturers of the <a href="/wiki/Gold_Coast_Titans" title="Gold Coast Titans">Gold Coast Titans</a> Rugby League club in the Australasian <a href="/wiki/National_Rugby_League" title="National Rugby League">National Rugby League</a>. Dual rugby and league international and former boxer <a href="/wiki/Sonny_Bill_Williams" title="Sonny Bill Williams">Sonny Bill Williams</a> is a global ambassador for Adidas.\n</p><p>Adidas has provided <a href="/wiki/Field_hockey" title="Field hockey">field hockey</a> equipment and sponsors numerous players of Germany, England, Netherlands, Australia, Spain and Belgium. The company has been the kit provider of Argentine <a href="/wiki/Argentina_women%27s_national_field_hockey_team" title="Argentina women&#39;s national field hockey team">women\'s</a> and <a href="/wiki/Argentina_men%27s_national_field_hockey_team" title="Argentina men&#39;s national field hockey team">men\'s</a> teams for over 15 years.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> The company also sponsored clubs <a href="/wiki/Reading_Hockey_Club" title="Reading Hockey Club">Reading</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Beeston_Hockey_Club" title="Beeston Hockey Club">Beeston</a><sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/East_Grinstead_Hockey_Club" title="East Grinstead Hockey Club">East Grinstead</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/Ice_hockey" title="Ice hockey">ice hockey</a>, Adidas signed an agreement with <a href="/wiki/National_Hockey_League" title="National Hockey League">National Hockey League</a> (NHL) to be the official outfitter of uniforms and licensed apparel, starting in the 2017\xe2\x80\x9318 season. Adidas will replace its own subsidiary <a href="/wiki/Reebok" title="Reebok">Reebok</a> as official provider.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Adidas\' <a href="/wiki/Cricket" title="Cricket">cricket</a> sponsorships include cricketers <a href="/wiki/Lasith_Malinga" title="Lasith Malinga">Lasith Malinga</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kieron_Pollard" title="Kieron Pollard">Kieron Pollard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dwayne_Bravo" title="Dwayne Bravo">Dwayne Bravo</a> and <a href="/wiki/K._L._Rahul" title="K. L. Rahul">K. L. Rahul</a>.\nAdidas sponsorships <a href="/wiki/Ivan_Zaytsev_(volleyball)" title="Ivan Zaytsev (volleyball)">Ivan Zaytsev</a> volleyball player.\n<a href="/wiki/Earvin_N%27Gapeth" title="Earvin N&#39;Gapeth">Earvin N\'Gapeth</a> volleyball player it advertises as a model and brand ambassador for Adidas.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Rivalries">Rivalries</span></h2>\n<p>In 2016, it had filed lawsuits against <a href="/wiki/Skechers" title="Skechers">Skechers</a>, one for making a duplicate Stan Smith design, and another for Adidas replicas such as "Springblade".<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Corporate_information">Corporate information</span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Current_executive_board">Current executive board</span></h3>\n<ul><li>CEO: <a href="/wiki/Kasper_R%C3%B8rsted" title="Kasper R\xc3\xb8rsted">Kasper R\xc3\xb8rsted</a></li>\n<li>Chief Financial Officer: Harm Ohlmeyer</li>\n<li>Global Brands: Eric Liedtke</li>\n<li>Global Operations: Gil Steyeart</li>\n<li>Global Sales: Roland Auschel</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Former_management">Former management</span></h3>\n<ul><li>CEO (1993\xe2\x80\x932002): <a href="/wiki/Robert_Louis-Dreyfus" title="Robert Louis-Dreyfus">Robert Louis-Dreyfus</a>.</li>\n<li>CEO (2002\xe2\x80\x932016): <a href="/wiki/Herbert_Hainer" title="Herbert Hainer">Herbert Hainer</a></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Financial_information">Financial information</span></h3>\n<table class="wikitable">\n<caption><b>Financial data in millions of euros</b><sup id="cite_ref-AR2016_95-0" class="reference"><a debt</a>\n</td>\n<td>2,231\n</td>\n<td>1,766\n</td>\n<td>2,189\n</td>\n<td>917\n</td>\n<td>221\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Criticism">Criticism</span></h2>\n<p>Adidas\'s business practises/<a href="/wiki/Ethics" title="Ethics">ethics</a> and commitment to worker welfare have been scrutinised and often criticised.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2011_All_Blacks_replica_rugby_jersey_pricing_controversy">2011 All Blacks replica rugby jersey pricing controversy</span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:All_blacks_jersey_whitebackg.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/All_blacks_jersey_whitebackg.jpg/200px-All_blacks_jersey_whitebackg.jpg" width="200" height="162" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/All_blacks_jersey_whitebackg.jpg/300px-All_blacks_jersey_whitebackg.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/All_blacks_jersey_whitebackg.jpg/400px-All_blacks_jersey_whitebackg.jpg 2x" data-file-width="884" data-file-height="714" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:All_blacks_jersey_whitebackg.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The All Blacks jersey caused controversy</div></div></div>\n<p>Unhappy with the local price of the Adidas replica All Blacks jersey, New Zealand-based <a href="/wiki/All_Blacks" class="mw-redirect" title="All Blacks">All Blacks</a> fans have asked for price cuts and begun purchasing the jersey from overseas vendors after it was revealed that the local price of $NZ220 was more than twice the price offered on some websites.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Adidas has responded by enforcing cross-border agreements to stop overseas retailers from selling to New Zealand residents. It has been labelled a public relations disaster by leading New Zealand PR firms and Consumer advocate groups. The largest New Zealand sportswear retailer <a href="/wiki/Rebel_Sport" title="Rebel Sport">Rebel Sport</a> has stated it is angry and is considering selling the All Blacks Jerseys to the general public below cost.\n</p>\n<h3><span id="2012_.22shackle.22_sneakers"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2012_&quot;shackle&quot;_sneakers">2012 "shackle" sneakers</span></h3>\n<p>On 14 June 2012, Adidas posted on their Facebook page a picture of a pair of <a href="/wiki/Jeremy_Scott" title="Jeremy Scott">Jeremy Scott</a>-designed shoes containing shackles. The picture was of a planned shoe line that Adidas intended to release in July. The photo quickly caused controversy including that of <a href="/wiki/Jesse_Jackson" title="Jesse Jackson">Jesse Jackson</a> who was quoted as saying "The attempt to commercialize and make popular more than 200 years of human degradation, where blacks were considered three-fifths human by our Constitution is offensive, appalling and insensitive".<sup id="cite_ref-Shackles_99-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shackles-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> Jackson threatened a boycott, and NBA commissioner <a href="/wiki/David_Stern" title="David Stern">David Stern</a> was at one point reportedly contacted in hopes that he would intervene.<sup id="cite_ref-Shackles_99-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shackles-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> Shortly after the outcry, the company cancelled the product.<sup id="cite_ref-Shackles_99-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shackles-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sweatshops_and_labour_rights_violations">Sweatshops and labour rights violations</span></h3>\n<p>Adidas has been criticized for operating <a href="/wiki/Sweatshops" class="mw-redirect" title="Sweatshops">sweatshops</a>, particularly in Indonesia. Between 2006 and 2007, Adidas rejected many of its suppliers that supported unions for subcontractors with less reputable labour rights records.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> By subcontracting work to different suppliers, it is more difficult for Adidas to ensure company labour standards are enforced. Workplace standards that Adidas\' policy upholds include the freedom for workers to take part in <a href="/wiki/Collective_bargaining" title="Collective bargaining">collective bargaining</a> and a non-retaliation policy towards workers who express concerns.<sup id="cite_ref-sustainability_101-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sustainability-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> In practice, however, many of Adidas\' suppliers have not upheld these standards. At the Panarub factory in <a href="/wiki/Java" title="Java">Java</a>, 33 workers were fired after striking for better pay in 2005.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> PT Kizone is another Indonesian factory where Adidas has received criticism over treatment of workers. They produced products for Adidas as well as <a href="/wiki/Nike,_Inc." title="Nike, Inc.">Nike</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Dallas_Cowboys" title="Dallas Cowboys">Dallas Cowboys</a> until they closed in January 2011. 2,686 workers who were laid off are owed $3 million in severance pay and benefits. Nike has contributed $1.5 million but Adidas has not acted. A campaign has been initiated by United Students Against Sweatshops calling for universities to cut contracts with Adidas.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> On 16 July 2012, <a href="/wiki/War_on_Want" title="War on Want">War on Want</a> organised activists in London to replace Adidas price tags in sports stores with 34p ones,<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> a reference to the low hourly wage rate paid to the Indonesian workers who make Adidas goods.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> The campaign group <a href="/wiki/Labour_Behind_the_Label" title="Labour Behind the Label">Labour Behind the Label</a> claimed that the basic pay of Indonesian Adidas workers was only \xc2\xa310 a week. William Anderson, head of social and environmental affairs for the Asia Pacific region, posted an entry on the company blog in which he sought to justify the 34p an hour pay rate.<sup id="cite_ref-poverty_106-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-poverty-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In April 2014, one of the biggest strikes on mainland <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> took place at the <a href="/wiki/Yue_Yuen_Industrial_Holdings" title="Yue Yuen Industrial Holdings">Yue Yuen Industrial Holdings</a> Dongguan shoe factory, producing amongst others for Adidas.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Environmental_record">Environmental record</span></h3>\n<p>For years, Adidas purchased paper for its packaging from <a href="/wiki/Asia_Pulp_%26_Paper" title="Asia Pulp &amp; Paper">Asia Pulp &amp; Paper</a>, the third largest paper producer in the world, which was labeled<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Words_to_watch#Unsupported_attributions" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Words to watch"><span title="The material near this tag may use weasel words or too-vague attribution. (July 2017)">by whom?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> as a "forest criminal" for destroying "precious habitat" in Indonesia\'s rainforest.<sup id="cite_ref-Paper_Giant_Pledges_to_Leave_the_Poor_Rainforest_Alone._Finally._Asia_Pulp_&amp;_Paper\xe2\x80\x94the_notorious_destroyer_of_pristine_tiger_and_orangutan_habitat\xe2\x80\x94says_it&#39;s_changing_its_ways._108-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Paper_Giant_Pledges_to_Leave_the_Poor_Rainforest_Alone._Finally._Asia_Pulp_&amp;_Paper\xe2\x80\x94the_notorious_destroyer_of_pristine_tiger_and_orangutan_habitat\xe2\x80\x94says_it&#39;s_changing_its_ways.-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> In 2011, when Adidas cancelled its contract with <a href="/wiki/Asia_Pulp_%26_Paper" title="Asia Pulp &amp; Paper">Asia Pulp &amp; Paper</a>, <a href="/wiki/Greenpeace" title="Greenpeace">Greenpeace</a> Executive Director <a href="/wiki/Phil_Radford" title="Phil Radford">Phil Radford</a> commended Adidas for efforts made towards forest protection, for "taking rainforest conservation seriously."<sup id="cite_ref-Hasbro_Turns_Over_a_New_Leaf,_Steps_Up_for_Rainforests_109-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hasbro_Turns_Over_a_New_Leaf,_Steps_Up_for_Rainforests-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="NCAA_corruption_scandal">NCAA corruption scandal</span></h3>\n<p>Adidas executive James Gatto has been indicted in the <a href="/wiki/2017_NCAA_Division_I_men%27s_basketball_corruption_scandal" class="mw-redirect" title="2017 NCAA Division I men&#39;s basketball corruption scandal">2017 NCAA Division I men\'s basketball corruption scandal</a>.\n<sup id="cite_ref-espn-schlabach_110-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espn-schlabach-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-nbcnews_111-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nbcnews-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-sbnation_112-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbnation-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span></h2>\n<div role="navigation" aria-label="Portals"
